Inventory at the end of the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">2013</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;totaled </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$163.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;compared to $125.4 million at the end of the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">2012</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">. The Company ended the quarter with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">226</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;stores in North America and Australia.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Christine Day, lululemon's CEO, stated: "2013 continues to be the most important and most productive year in lululemon's history.&#160;We have not only worked our way back from the black luon setback, but have also added very talented people in important functions and have taken major steps forward on a number of key fronts including the expansion of our international and men's businesses and many logistical initiatives. In addition, our exclusive partnership with Noble announced today and additional sources for luon will help to ensure that lululemon remains a distinct leader in quality and innovation." Ms. Day continues: "We are well on our way to finishing 2013 as a much stronger company than when the year began. I am confident that the leadership currently in place coupled with a new CEO will have tremendous success leveraging the platform for growth."</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Creating components for people to live long, healthy and fun lives</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s41b816fa844c40aa8bdf88d622718bb4"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;"><img src="g551549img001.jpg" style="height:62px;width:365px;"></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Strategic global alliance with Noble Biomaterials</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Today we announced a strategic global alliance for X-STATIC&#174; with Noble Biomaterials. The partnership gives lululemon exclusivity to use Noble's X-STATIC&#174; antimicrobial technology in our performance apparel. Noble has been a longstanding partner of lululemon, providing its X-STATIC&#174; technology for our Silverescent&#174; fabric since 2005. This unique opportunity allows us to continue to innovate our technical product with X-STATIC&#174; and secure our leadership position in &#8220;anti-stink&#8221; athletic apparel. X-STATIC&#174;'s properties have helped lululemon to set the industry standard by using the most powerful silver fabric technology to create our Silverescent&#174; fabrics. Made with 99.9% pure metallic silver, X-STATIC&#174; is designed to provide permanent odor protection by naturally inhibiting the growth of bacteria on the surface of fabrics. The silver fiber is woven directly into the garment and will not wash out over time through laundering.</font></div><a name="saebec051184d417fa3110f505ea4e492"></a><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Updated Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">For the third quarter of fiscal 2013, we expect net revenue to be in the range of $370 million to $375 million based on a comparable-store sales percentage increase in the mid-single digits on a constant-dollar basis. Diluted earnings per share are expected to be in the range of $0.39 to $0.41 for the quarter. This assumes 146.0&#160;million diluted weighted-average shares outstanding and a tax rate of 30.0%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">For the full fiscal 2013, we now expect net revenue to be in the range of $1.625 billion to $1.635 billion and diluted earnings per share are expected to be in the range of $1.94 to $1.97 for the full year. This assumes 146.0&#160;million diluted weighted-average shares outstanding and a tax rate of 30.0%.</font></div><a name="sf053afb7a1a444bc8b3169db5bbe7277"></a><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:18px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call Information</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">A conference call to discuss second quarter results is scheduled for today, September&#160;12, 2013, at 9:00 a.m. EST. Those interested in participating in the call are invited to dial 1-877-303-3203 approximately 10 minutes prior to the start of the call. The conference call will also be webcast live at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:underline;">www.lululemon.com</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">. The webcast will be accessible on our website for approximately 30 days after the call.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:18px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">About lululemon athletica inc.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">lululemon athletica (NASDAQ:LULU) is a yoga-inspired athletic apparel company that creates components for people to live long, healthy and fun lives.&#160;By producing products that help keep people active and stress free, lululemon believes that the world will be a better place. Setting the bar in technical fabrics and functional designs, lululemon works with yogis and athletes in local communities for continuous research and product feedback.&#160;For more information, visit </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:underline;">www.lululemon.com</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:18px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measure</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Constant-dollar net revenue changes, which exclude the impact of changes in foreign exchange rates, is not a United States Generally Accepted Accounting Principle (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;) performance measure. We provide constant-dollar net revenue changes because we use the measure to understand the underlying growth rate of revenue excluding the impact on a quarter-by-quarter basis of changes in foreign exchange rates, which are not under management&#8217;s direct control. We believe that disclosing net revenue changes on a constant-dollar basis is useful to investors because it enables them to better understand the level of growth of our business.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The presentation of this financial information is not intended to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for, or superior to, the financial information prepared and presented in accordance with GAAP. For more information on this non-GAAP financial measure, please see the table captioned &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measure &#8211; Constant dollar changes&#8221; included in the accompanying financial tables, which includes more detail on the GAAP financial measure that is most directly comparable to non-GAAP financial measures and the related reconciliations between these financial measures.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:18px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">This press release contains &#8220;forward-looking statements&#8221;
